<initial_plan>
1) {hard_constraints}
    *   Trip duration: 5 days
    *   Destination: Europe
    *   Budget: Approximately €1,700 (total cost for flights, accommodation, restaurants, and activities)
    *   Type of trip: Family vacation

2) {soft_constraints}
    *   Matching user's interests for activities and restaurant preferences. This will require input from the external agent.
    *   The budget of €1,700 is a target, allowing for slight flexibility if a better value or experience is offered close to this amount.

3) {task_decomposition}
    *   **Sub-task 1: Gather Core Trip Details from External Agent**
        *   Identify the specific European destination (city/country).
        *   Determine the exact 5-day travel dates.
        *   Confirm the number of family members traveling (adults and children, including ages if applicable).
        *   Inquire about any specific interests for activities (e.g., historical sites, nature, museums, adventure, relaxation).
        *   Ask about preferred restaurant types or cuisines and any dietary restrictions.
    *   **Sub-task 2: Research and Propose Initial Options (with External Agent)**
        *   **Flights:** Research flight options to the chosen destination for the specified dates, considering the budget and family size. Obtain estimated costs.
        *   **Accommodation:** Research family-friendly hotel or rental options within the budget for the chosen destination and dates. Obtain estimated costs.
        *   **Activities:** Based on the user's interests and destination, propose a selection of 5-day activities. Obtain estimated costs.
        *   **Restaurants:** Suggest types of restaurants or specific dining experiences based on preferences. Estimate daily food costs.
    *   **Sub-task 3: Refine and Confirm Plan (with External Agent)**
        *   Present the proposed itinerary including flights, accommodation, activities, and estimated restaurant costs to the external agent for review and feedback.
        *   Adjust proposals based on feedback and ensure adherence to the budget.
        *   Secure confirmations for all bookings (flights, accommodation, chosen activities).
    *   **Sub-task 4: Compile Final Budget Breakdown**
        *   Document the confirmed destination, travel dates, exact costs for transportation (flights), accommodation, activities, estimated restaurant costs, and any additional services.
        *   Calculate the total confirmed budget.

4) {data_planning}
    *   **From External Agent (Travel Agency):**
        *   Preferred European destination (specific city/country).
        *   Specific 5-day travel dates.
        *   Number of travelers (adults and children with ages).
        *   Specific interests for activities.
        *   Restaurant preferences/dietary restrictions.
        *   Approval/feedback on proposed itinerary components.
    *   **From Environment:**
        *   User's name (for personalization, if needed).
        *   User's calendar availability (if the external agent is flexible on dates or asks for user's availability).
        *   User's family members (if available, to cross-reference family size/ages, though I will primarily ask the external agent).

5) {anticipated_changes}
    *   **Destination:** The external agent might have a specific European city in mind, or I may need to propose options.
    *   **Travel Dates:** The external agent might provide exact dates, or I may need to suggest dates and check user calendar availability if flexibility is indicated.
    *   **Budget Allocation:** The breakdown of the €1,700 budget across flights, accommodation, activities, and food can be flexible, as long as the total remains around the target.
    *   **Interests/Preferences:** The specific activities and restaurant choices will be highly dependent on the external agent's input and may require multiple iterations of suggestions.
    *   **Availability:** Initial flight or accommodation options might not be available for the preferred dates/prices, requiring alternative searches.
</initial_plan>
